aria-label="Hide sidebar navigation" class="Nav-toggle-collapse39KxgTH727KL" type="button"></button></nav><article class="SuperHubDoc-article3ArTrEavUTKg rm-Article rm-Guides-SuperHub"><header id="content-head"><div class="row clearfix"><div class="col-xs-9"><h1>Desktop Application</h1></div></div></header><div class="grid-container-fluid" id="content-container"><section class="content-body grid-75 "><div dehydrated="&lt;p&gt;The Desktop Application is designed to work across Windows and macOS. It enables access to various targets using native clients such as database clients, SSH terminals, or RDP software.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Who benefits from using this application?&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;IT Administrators and DevOps Teams&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Security Professionals&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Developers and Engineers&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;blockquote class=&quot;callout callout_info&quot; theme=&quot;ℹ️&quot;&gt;&lt;h2 class=&quot;callout-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;callout-icon&quot;&gt;ℹ️&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Desktop Application is currently in beta.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;h2 class=&quot;heading heading-2 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;prerequisites&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-prerequisites&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;Prerequisites&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to Prerequisites&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#prerequisites&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Windows&lt;/strong&gt; or &lt;strong&gt;macOS Ventura&lt;/strong&gt; / &lt;strong&gt;Monterey&lt;/strong&gt; / &lt;strong&gt;Big Sur&lt;/strong&gt; operating system.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h3 class=&quot;heading heading-3 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;permissions&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-permissions&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;Permissions&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to Permissions&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#permissions&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The Desktop Application creates a tunnel to the designated resource and securely injects the password. To support this process, any user working with the Desktop Application must have &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.akeyless.io/docs/rbac#permissions-for-items-access-roles-auth-methods-and-targets&quot; target=&quot;&quot; title=&quot;&quot;&gt;read permission&lt;/a&gt; on the Secret Item.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h2 class=&quot;heading heading-2 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;installation-guide&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-installation-guide&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;Installation Guide&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to Installation Guide&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#installation-guide&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Download the relevant Desktop Application installer from (&lt;a href=&quot;https://download.akeyless.io/Akeyless_Artifacts/&quot; target=&quot;&quot; title=&quot;&quot;&gt;https://download.akeyless.io/Akeyless_Artifacts/&lt;/a&gt;).&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;h3 class=&quot;heading heading-3 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;windows-installation&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-windows-installation&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;Windows Installation&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to Windows Installation&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#windows-installation&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ol&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Open Windows Command Prompt as an administrator and generate private and public SSH keys locally. You can use the following command: &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;ssh-keygen -t rsa&lt;/code&gt;. This creates an &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;.ssh&lt;/code&gt; folder with the &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;id_rsa&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;id_rsa.pub&lt;/code&gt; files.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Run the &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;.exe&lt;/code&gt; file and follow the setup wizard.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Grant necessary permissions if prompted.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The Desktop Application installs at &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;C:/Users/&amp;lt;username&amp;gt;/AppData/Roaming/Akeyless-desktop&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Open the app and sign in with your Akeyless credentials.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;
&lt;h3 class=&quot;heading heading-3 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;macos-installation&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-mac-os-installation&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;macOS Installation&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to macOS Installation&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#macos-installation&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ol&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;After downloading the appropriate installer file, locate it in your &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;Downloads&lt;/code&gt; folder or the directory you specified.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Open it and drag the Akeyless Remote Access app to the Applications folder.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Grant required permissions in &lt;strong&gt;System Preferences&lt;/strong&gt; → &lt;strong&gt;Security &amp;amp; Privacy&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The Desktop Application installs at &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;~/Library/Application Support/Akeyless-Desktop&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Open the app and sign in with your Akeyless credentials.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;
&lt;blockquote class=&quot;callout callout_info&quot; theme=&quot;ℹ️&quot;&gt;&lt;h2 class=&quot;callout-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;callout-icon&quot;&gt;ℹ️&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note (Installation Folder):&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;The installation folder contains the following:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;ol&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;config.json&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; - The configuration file (contains the basic parameters required to launch the Desktop Application). This file can be deployed by an admin across the organization.
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;ol&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Logs&lt;/strong&gt; - Located at &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;Akeyless-desktop/logs&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;
&lt;h2 class=&quot;heading heading-2 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;how-it-works&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-how-it-works&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;How It Works&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to How It Works&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#how-it-works&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ol&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;The Desktop Application retrieves connection details from the target item (For example, &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;MY-MSSQL-connection&lt;/code&gt;) and initiates a connection.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;It uses the Akeyless CLI to establish a tunnel, leveraging the SSH certificate configured in the &lt;strong&gt;Defaults Configuration&lt;/strong&gt; window.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote class=&quot;callout callout_warn&quot; theme=&quot;⚠️&quot;&gt;&lt;h2 class=&quot;callout-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;callout-icon&quot;&gt;⚠️&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Warning (Important):&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;ol&gt;
&lt;li&gt;If you don&amp;#x27;t have an SSH certificate yet, please follow this guide on creating an &lt;a href=&quot;https://docs.akeyless.io/docs/ssh-certificates&quot; target=&quot;&quot; title=&quot;&quot;&gt;SSH Cert issuer&lt;/a&gt; with Akeyless and set your &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;CAPublicKey&lt;/code&gt; in the &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;values&lt;/code&gt; file.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;You also need to enable Secure Remote Access on the SSH Cert Issuer either in the UI or by adding the &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;--secure-access-enable true&lt;/code&gt; flag to your CLI command.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Ensure that the &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;akeyless&lt;/code&gt; user is added to the list of &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;Allowed User(s)&lt;/code&gt; in the SSH Cert Issuer item. Otherwise, the desktop application will not be able to establish a connection.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Upon successfully connecting to the remote target, the Desktop Application launches the default application configured for this resource type.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;
&lt;blockquote class=&quot;callout callout_info&quot; theme=&quot;ℹ️&quot;&gt;&lt;h2 class=&quot;callout-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;callout-icon&quot;&gt;ℹ️&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;Applications such as &lt;strong&gt;Azure Data Studio&lt;/strong&gt;, &lt;strong&gt;Windows App&lt;/strong&gt;, &lt;strong&gt;DBeaver&lt;/strong&gt;, &lt;strong&gt;PuTTY&lt;/strong&gt;, &lt;strong&gt;WinSCP&lt;/strong&gt;, and others should already be installed on the local machine where the desktop application is installed.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;h2 class=&quot;heading heading-2 header-scroll&quot; align=&quot;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-anchor anchor waypoint&quot; id=&quot;configuration--first-time-setup&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;heading-text&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;section-configuration-first-time-setup&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;Configuration &amp;amp; First-Time Setup&lt;/div&gt;&lt;a aria-label=&quot;Skip link to Configuration &amp;amp; First-Time Setup&quot; class=&quot;heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor&quot; href=&quot;#configuration--first-time-setup&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ol&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Log in to the Desktop Application (using SAML, OIDC, Certificate, Access Key, and so on). You should see a list of the resources you can connect to based on your permissions. If you want to add or remove targets from the list, update your permissions accordingly.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Application Mapping&lt;/strong&gt; - To connect to remote resources, users should map them to applications. When using a mapped application, the desktop application launches the native application and securely initiates the connection.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Listed below are the native clients that are supported by the Desktop Application:&lt;/p&gt;





































































































&lt;div class=&quot;rdmd-table&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;rdmd-table-inner&quot;&gt;&lt;table&gt;&lt;thead&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Operating System&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Resource&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Application Type&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Comments&lt;/th&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/thead&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Windows&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;MSSQL Server&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Azure Data Studio&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;RDP&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Remote Desktop&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Postgres DB&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;DBeaver&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;SSH Cert Issuer&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;PuTTY&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;WinSCP is a prerequisite for PuTTY.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;SSH username and password&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;PuTTY&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Specify port &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;2022&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;SSH File Transfer&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;WinSCP&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Note: File transfers for certificate-based targets have a known limitation and are currently not supported.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;PowerShell&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;PuTTY&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;PS tag should be configured on the secret item.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Direct Connection and Secure Remote Access&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Default Browser&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;strong&gt;macOS&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;MSSQL Server&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Azure Data Studio&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Postgres DB&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;DBeaver&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;RDP&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Windows App&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;SSH Cert Issuer&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Terminal&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;SSH username and password&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Terminal&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Direct Connection and Secure Remote Access&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Default Browser&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;SSH File Transfer (SFTP)&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Terminal&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;blockquote class=&quot;callout callout_warn&quot; theme=&quot;⚠️&quot;&gt;&lt;h2 class=&quot;callout-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;callout-icon&quot;&gt;⚠️&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Warning (Multiple hosts and linked targets):&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Desktop Application supports multiple hosts and linked targets. You can add or remove hosts you want to connect to, and then select &lt;strong&gt;Confirm&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Removing a host from the list only removes it from the Desktop Application host list.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Configure the &lt;strong&gt;Defaults Configuration&lt;/strong&gt; - When connecting to a remote target, the Desktop Application fetches the required parameters from the resource item (the target you want to connect to). If this information is not accessible to the Desktop Application, it uses the information configured in Advanced Configuration.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Web Application Dispatcher&lt;/strong&gt; and &lt;strong&gt;Web Proxy URL&lt;/strong&gt; - Should be provided if working with the Zero Trust Web Access solution (ZTWA).&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Secure SSH Access Address&lt;/strong&gt; (recommended) - This is the path and port for SSH deployment (&lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;my.SSH.address&lt;/code&gt;).&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;SSH Certificate Issuer&lt;/strong&gt; (recommended) - This is the name of the SSH Certificate Issuer that the Akeyless CLI uses to initiate the connection.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Control API Port&lt;/strong&gt; - The control API port (specify &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;8000&lt;/code&gt; for a unified Gateway, or &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;9900&lt;/code&gt; otherwise).&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Control API Path&lt;/strong&gt; - The SRA control API path (for example, &lt;button aria-label=&quot;Copy Code&quot; class=&quot;rdmd-code-copy fa&quot;&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;code class=&quot;rdmd-code lang- theme-light&quot; data-lang=&quot;&quot; name=&quot;&quot; tabindex=&quot;0&quot;&gt;/sra/ssh-config&lt;/code&gt;).&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;
&lt;blockquote class=&quot;callout callout_info&quot; theme=&quot;ℹ️&quot;&gt;&lt;h2 class=&quot;callout-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;callout-icon&quot;&gt;ℹ️&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note (Connection Failures):&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;If the desktop application fails to connect to the resource, it will display a message prompting you to verify your configuration.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The Desktop log contains additional information that can help during an investigation.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/blockquote&gt;" style="margin-left:31px" class="rm-Markdown markdown-body rm-Markdown markdown-body ng-non-bindable" data-testid="RDMD"><p>The Desktop Application is designed to work across Windows and macOS. It enables access to various targets using native clients such as database clients, SSH terminals, or RDP software.</p>
<p>Who benefits from using this application?</p>
<ul>
<li>IT Administrators and DevOps Teams</li>
<li>Security Professionals</li>
<li>Developers and Engineers</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="callout callout_info" theme="ℹ️"><h2 class="callout-heading"><span class="callout-icon">ℹ️</span><p><strong>Note:</strong></p></h2><p>The Desktop Application is currently in beta.</p></blockquote>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="prerequisites"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-prerequisites" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Prerequisites</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Prerequisites" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#prerequisites"></a></h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Windows</strong> or <strong>macOS Ventura</strong> / <strong>Monterey</strong> / <strong>Big Sur</strong> operating system.</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="permissions"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-permissions" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Permissions</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Permissions" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#permissions"></a></h3>
<p>The Desktop Application creates a tunnel to the designated resource and securely injects the password. To support this process, any user working with the Desktop Application must have <a target="_self" href="/docs/rbac#permissions-for-items-access-roles-auth-methods-and-targets">read permission</a> on the Secret Item.</p>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="installation-guide"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-installation-guide" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Installation Guide</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Installation Guide" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#installation-guide"></a></h2>
<p>Download the relevant Desktop Application installer from (<a target="_self" href="https://download.akeyless.io/Akeyless_Artifacts/">https://download.akeyless.io/Akeyless_Artifacts/</a>).</p>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="windows-installation"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-windows-installation" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Windows Installation</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Windows Installation" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#windows-installation"></a></h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Open Windows Command Prompt as an administrator and generate private and public SSH keys locally. You can use the following command: <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">ssh-keygen -t rsa</code>. This creates an <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">.ssh</code> folder with the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">id_rsa</code> and <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">id_rsa.pub</code> files.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Run the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">.exe</code> file and follow the setup wizard.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Grant necessary permissions if prompted.</p>
<p>The Desktop Application installs at <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">C:/Users/&lt;username&gt;/AppData/Roaming/Akeyless-desktop</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Open the app and sign in with your Akeyless credentials.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="macos-installation"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-mac-os-installation" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>macOS Installation</div><a aria-label="Skip link to macOS Installation" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#macos-installation"></a></h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p>After downloading the appropriate installer file, locate it in your <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">Downloads</code> folder or the directory you specified.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Open it and drag the Akeyless Remote Access app to the Applications folder.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Grant required permissions in <strong>System Preferences</strong> → <strong>Security &amp; Privacy</strong>.</p>
<p>The Desktop Application installs at <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">~/Library/Application Support/Akeyless-Desktop</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Open the app and sign in with your Akeyless credentials.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote class="callout callout_info" theme="ℹ️"><h2 class="callout-heading"><span class="callout-icon">ℹ️</span><p><strong>Note (Installation Folder):</strong></p></h2><p>The installation folder contains the following:</p></blockquote>
<ol>
<li><strong><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">config.json</code></strong> - The configuration file (contains the basic parameters required to launch the Desktop Application). This file can be deployed by an admin across the organization.
<blockquote>
<ol>
<li><strong>Logs</strong> - Located at <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">Akeyless-desktop/logs</code>.</li>
</ol>
</blockquote>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="how-it-works"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-how-it-works" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>How It Works</div><a aria-label="Skip link to How It Works" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#how-it-works"></a></h2>
<ol>
<li>
<p>The Desktop Application retrieves connection details from the target item (For example, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">MY-MSSQL-connection</code>) and initiates a connection.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It uses the Akeyless CLI to establish a tunnel, leveraging the SSH certificate configured in the <strong>Defaults Configuration</strong> window.</p>
<blockquote class="callout callout_warn" theme="⚠️"><h2 class="callout-heading"><span class="callout-icon">⚠️</span><p><strong>Warning (Important):</strong></p></h2><ol>
<li>If you don&#x27;t have an SSH certificate yet, please follow this guide on creating an <a target="_self" href="/docs/ssh-certificates">SSH Cert issuer</a> with Akeyless and set your <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">CAPublicKey</code> in the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">values</code> file.</li>
<li>You also need to enable Secure Remote Access on the SSH Cert Issuer either in the UI or by adding the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">--secure-access-enable true</code> flag to your CLI command.</li>
<li>Ensure that the <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">akeyless</code> user is added to the list of <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">Allowed User(s)</code> in the SSH Cert Issuer item. Otherwise, the desktop application will not be able to establish a connection.</li>
</ol></blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p>Upon successfully connecting to the remote target, the Desktop Application launches the default application configured for this resource type.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote class="callout callout_info" theme="ℹ️"><h2 class="callout-heading"><span class="callout-icon">ℹ️</span><p><strong>Note:</strong></p></h2><p>Applications such as <strong>Azure Data Studio</strong>, <strong>Windows App</strong>, <strong>DBeaver</strong>, <strong>PuTTY</strong>, <strong>WinSCP</strong>, and others should already be installed on the local machine where the desktop application is installed.</p></blockquote>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="configuration--first-time-setup"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-configuration-first-time-setup" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Configuration &amp; First-Time Setup</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Configuration &amp; First-Time Setup" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#configuration--first-time-setup"></a></h2>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Log in to the Desktop Application (using SAML, OIDC, Certificate, Access Key, and so on). You should see a list of the resources you can connect to based on your permissions. If you want to add or remove targets from the list, update your permissions accordingly.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Application Mapping</strong> - To connect to remote resources, users should map them to applications. When using a mapped application, the desktop application launches the native application and securely initiates the connection.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Listed below are the native clients that are supported by the Desktop Application:</p>





































































































<div class="rdmd-table"><div class="rdmd-table-inner"><table><thead><tr><th>Operating System</th><th>Resource</th><th>Application Type</th><th>Comments</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><strong>Windows</strong></td><td>MSSQL Server</td><td>Azure Data Studio</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>RDP</td><td>Remote Desktop</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>Postgres DB</td><td>DBeaver</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>SSH Cert Issuer</td><td>PuTTY</td><td>WinSCP is a prerequisite for PuTTY.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>SSH username and password</td><td>PuTTY</td><td>Specify port <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">2022</code>.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>SSH File Transfer</td><td>WinSCP</td><td>Note: File transfers for certificate-based targets have a known limitation and are currently not supported.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>PowerShell</td><td>PuTTY</td><td>PS tag should be configured on the secret item.</td></tr><tr><td></td><td>Direct Connection and Secure Remote Access</td><td>Default Browser</td><td></td></tr><tr><td><strong>macOS</strong></td><td>MSSQL Server</td><td>Azure Data Studio</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>Postgres DB</td><td>DBeaver</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>RDP</td><td>Windows App</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>SSH Cert Issuer</td><td>Terminal</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>SSH username and password</td><td>Terminal</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>Direct Connection and Secure Remote Access</td><td>Default Browser</td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td>SSH File Transfer (SFTP)</td><td>Terminal</td><td></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>
<blockquote class="callout callout_warn" theme="⚠️"><h2 class="callout-heading"><span class="callout-icon">⚠️</span><p><strong>Warning (Multiple hosts and linked targets):</strong></p></h2><p>The Desktop Application supports multiple hosts and linked targets. You can add or remove hosts you want to connect to, and then select <strong>Confirm</strong>.</p><p>Removing a host from the list only removes it from the Desktop Application host list.</p></blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p>Configure the <strong>Defaults Configuration</strong> - When connecting to a remote target, the Desktop Application fetches the required parameters from the resource item (the target you want to connect to). If this information is not accessible to the Desktop Application, it uses the information configured in Advanced Configuration.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Web Application Dispatcher</strong> and <strong>Web Proxy URL</strong> - Should be provided if working with the Zero Trust Web Access solution (ZTWA).</li>
<li><strong>Secure SSH Access Address</strong> (recommended) - This is the path and port for SSH deployment (<button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">my.SSH.address</code>).</li>
<li><strong>SSH Certificate Issuer</strong> (recommended) - This is the name of the SSH Certificate Issuer that the Akeyless CLI uses to initiate the connection.</li>
<li><strong>Control API Port</strong> - The control API port (specify <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">8000</code> for a unified Gateway, or <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">9900</code> otherwise).</li>
<li><strong>Control API Path</strong> - The SRA control API path (for example, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">/sra/ssh-config</code>).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<blockquote class="callout callout_info" theme="ℹ️"><h2 class="callout-heading"><span class="callout-icon">ℹ️</span><p><strong>Note (Connection Failures):</strong></p></h2><p>If the desktop application fails to connect to the resource, it will display a message prompting you to verify your configuration.</p><p>The Desktop log contains additional information that can help during an investigation.</p></blockquote></div><div align="center" class="Flex Flex_row " justify="between" style="--flex-gap:var(--md)"><div class="UpdatedAt"><p class="DateLine "><i class="icon icon-watch"></i>Updated<!-- --> <!-- -->4 days ago<!-- --> </p></div></div><hr class="NextStepsDivider"/><nav aria-label="Pagination Controls" class="PaginationControlsjDYuqu8pBMUy rm-Pagination"><a Application","type":"basic","updated_at":"2026-03-10T11:54:58.000Z","uri":"/branches/1.0/guides/remote-access-desktop-application-beta","appearance":{"icon":{"name":null,"type":null}},"category":{"uri":"/branches/1.0/categories/guides/Secure Remote Access"},"href":{"dash":"https://dash.readme.com/project/akeyless/v1.0/docs/remote-access-desktop-application-beta","hub":"https://docs.akeyless.io/docs/remote-access-desktop-application-beta","github_url":null},"links":{"project":"/projects/me"},"parent":{"uri":"/branches/1.0/guides/user-guides"},"privacy":{"view":"public"},"project":{"name":"Akeyless Vaultless Platform","subdomain":"akeyless","uri":"/projects/me"},"content":{"body":"The Desktop Application is designed to work across Windows and macOS. It enables access to various targets using native clients such as database clients, SSH terminals, or RDP software.\n\nWho benefits from using this application?\n\n* IT Administrators and DevOps Teams\n* Security Professionals\n* Developers and Engineers\n\n> ℹ️ **Note:**\n>\n> The Desktop Application is currently in beta.\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n* **Windows** or **macOS Ventura** / **Monterey** / **Big Sur** operating system.\n\n### Permissions\n\nThe Desktop Application creates a tunnel to the designated resource and securely injects the password. To support this process, any user working with the Desktop Application must have [read permission](https://docs.akeyless.io/docs/rbac#permissions-for-items-access-roles-auth-methods-and-targets) on the Secret Item.\n\n## Installation Guide\n\nDownload the relevant Desktop Application installer from (\u003chttps://download.akeyless.io/Akeyless_Artifacts/>).\n\n### Windows Installation\n\n1. Open Windows Command Prompt as an administrator and generate private and public SSH keys locally. You can use the following command: `ssh-keygen -t rsa`. This creates an `.ssh` folder with the `id_rsa` and `id_rsa.pub` files.\n\n2. Run the `.exe` file and follow the setup wizard.\n\n3. Grant necessary permissions if prompted.\n\n    The Desktop Application installs at `C:/Users/\u003cusername>/AppData/Roaming/Akeyless-desktop`.\n\n4. Open the app and sign in with your Akeyless credentials.\n\n### macOS Installation\n\n1. After downloading the appropriate installer file, locate it in your `Downloads` folder or the directory you specified.\n\n2. Open it and drag the Akeyless Remote Access app to the Applications folder.\n\n3. Grant required permissions in **System Preferences** → **Security & Privacy**.\n\n    The Desktop Application installs at `~/Library/Application Support/Akeyless-Desktop`.\n\n4. Open the app and sign in with your Akeyless credentials.\n\n> ℹ️ **Note (Installation Folder):**\n>\n> The installation folder contains the following:\n>\n1. **`config.json`** - The configuration file (contains the basic parameters required to launch the Desktop Application). This file can be deployed by an admin across the organization.\n>\n> 1. **Logs** - Located at `Akeyless-desktop/logs`.\n\n## How It Works\n\n1. The Desktop Application retrieves connection details from the target item (For example, `MY-MSSQL-connection`) and initiates a connection.\n\n2. It uses the Akeyless CLI to establish a tunnel, leveraging the SSH certificate configured in the **Defaults Configuration** window.\n\n    > ⚠️ **Warning (Important):**\n    >\n    > 1. If you don't have an SSH certificate yet, please follow this guide on creating an [SSH Cert issuer](https://docs.akeyless.io/docs/ssh-certificates) with Akeyless and set your `CAPublicKey` in the `values` file.\n    > 2. You also need to enable Secure Remote Access on the SSH Cert Issuer either in the UI or by adding the `--secure-access-enable true` flag to your CLI command.\n    > 3. Ensure that the `akeyless` user is added to the list of `Allowed User(s)` in the SSH Cert Issuer item. Otherwise, the desktop application will not be able to establish a connection.\n\n3. Upon successfully connecting to the remote target, the Desktop Application launches the default application configured for this resource type.\n\n> ℹ️ **Note:**\n>\n> Applications such as **Azure Data Studio**, **Windows App**, **DBeaver**, **PuTTY**, **WinSCP**, and others should already be installed on the local machine where the desktop application is installed.\n\n## Configuration & First-Time Setup\n\n1. Log in to the Desktop Application (using SAML, OIDC, Certificate, Access Key, and so on). You should see a list of the resources you can connect to based on your permissions. If you want to add or remove targets from the list, update your permissions accordingly.\n2. **Application Mapping** - To connect to remote resources, users should map them to applications. When using a mapped application, the desktop application launches the native application and securely initiates the connection.\n3. Listed below are the native clients that are supported by the Desktop Application:\n\n    | Operating System | Resource | Application Type | Comments |\n    | --- | --- | --- | --- |\n    | **Windows** | MSSQL Server | Azure Data Studio |  |\n    |  | RDP | Remote Desktop |  |\n    |  | Postgres DB | DBeaver |  |\n    |  | SSH Cert Issuer | PuTTY | WinSCP is a prerequisite for PuTTY. |\n    |  | SSH username and password | PuTTY | Specify port `2022`. |\n    |  | SSH File Transfer | WinSCP | Note: File transfers for certificate-based targets have a known limitation and are currently not supported. |\n    |  | PowerShell | PuTTY | PS tag should be configured on the secret item. |\n    |  | Direct Connection and Secure Remote Access | Default Browser |  |\n    | **macOS** | MSSQL Server | Azure Data Studio |  |\n    |  | Postgres DB | DBeaver |  |\n    |  | RDP | Windows App |  |\n    |  | SSH Cert Issuer | Terminal |  |\n    |  | SSH username and password | Terminal |  |\n    |  | Direct Connection and Secure Remote Access | Default Browser |  |\n    |  | SSH File Transfer (SFTP) | Terminal |  |\n\n    > ⚠️ **Warning (Multiple hosts and linked targets):**\n    >\n    > The Desktop Application supports multiple hosts and linked targets. You can add or remove hosts you want to connect to, and then select **Confirm**.\n    >\n    > Removing a host from the list only removes it from the Desktop Application host list.\n\n4. Configure the **Defaults Configuration** - When connecting to a remote target, the Desktop Application fetches the required parameters from the resource item (the target you want to connect to). If this information is not accessible to the Desktop Application, it uses the information configured in Advanced Configuration.\n\n    * **Web Application Dispatcher** and **Web Proxy URL** - Should be provided if working with the Zero Trust Web Access solution (ZTWA).\n    * **Secure SSH Access Address** (recommended) - This is the path and port for SSH deployment (`my.SSH.address`).\n    * **SSH Certificate Issuer** (recommended) - This is the name of the SSH Certificate Issuer that the Akeyless CLI uses to initiate the connection.\n    * **Control API Port** - The control API port (specify `8000` for a unified Gateway, or `9900` otherwise).\n    * **Control API Path** - The SRA control API path (for example, `/sra/ssh-config`).\n\n> ℹ️ **Note (Connection Failures):**\n>\n> If the desktop application fails to connect to the resource, it will display a message prompting you to verify your configuration.\n>\n> The Desktop log contains additional information that can help during an investigation.","excerpt":null,"link":{"url":null,"new_tab":false},"next":{"description":null,"pages":[]}},"metadata":{"description":null,"keywords":null,"title":null,"image":{"uri":null,"url":null}}},"meta":{"baseUrl":"/","description":"The Desktop Application is designed to work across Windows and macOS. If you want to add or remove targets from the list, update your permissions accordingly.\u003c/p>\n\u003c/li>\n\u003cli>\n\u003cp>\u003cstrong>Application Mapping\u003c/strong> - To connect to remote resources, users should map them to applications.
